<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">after</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">make</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:namaken.html>namaken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to create <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>copies</a> or additional <a href = vnd.unilang:specimens.html>specimens</a> of <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">e.g. a spare</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:namelijk.html>namelijk</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>namely</li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Used to indicate that a statement explains an earlier one.</span>
<dl><dd><i>Franske <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kopen.html>kopen</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:namelijk.html>namelijk</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevraagd.html>gevraagd</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>Franske <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> to buy food <b>because</b> I asked him to.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">explanation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:immers.html>immers</a></span></li></ul>

***napoleon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:napoleon.html>napoleon</a> (5870)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">napoléon</i>. Named after <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Napoleon_Bonaparte" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Napoleon Bonaparte"><a href = vnd.unilang:napoleon.html>Napoleon</a> Bonaparte</a>, whose image the coins originally bore.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:napoleon.html>napoleon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:napoleons.html>napoleons</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> numismatics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The 20-franc gold coin, the <a href = vnd.unilang:franc.html>franc</a> germinal, originally issued under <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Napoleon_I_of_France" class="extiw" title="w:Napoleon I of France"><a href = vnd.unilang:napoleon.html>Napoleon</a></a>, but also used of subsequent gold coins of the same denomination.</li></ol>

</p>

***napraten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:napraten.html>napraten</a> (68558)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:praten.html>praten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:napraten.html>napraten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to say the same as, to copy</li>
<li>to talk lightly in private after a social event</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nazeggen.html>nazeggen</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***nasmaak.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nasmaak.html>nasmaak</a> (43356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">after-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smaak.html>smaak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">taste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>aftertaste
<ul><li><b>1781</b> October 31, S., "<a href = vnd.unilang:brief.html>Brief</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Heeren Schryveren <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Algemeene Vaderlandsche Letter-oeffeningen</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wegens.html>wegens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> nevensgaand Berigt <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruik.html>gebruik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eikels.html>Eikels</a>.", in <i>Algemeene Vaderlandsche Letter-oefeningen</i>, III, 2, 604.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">naz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">naz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nataz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ned-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nat.html>nat</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νοτέω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">notéō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νότος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nótos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the south wind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***natrium.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:natrium.html>natrium</a> (51179)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:natrium.html>Natrium</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:natrium.html>natrium</a></i>. Coined by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/J%C3%B6ns_Jacob_Berzelius" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jöns Jacob Berzelius">Jöns <a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> Berzelius</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:natrium.html>natrium</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>sodium (a reactive metal) <span class="defdate">[from 1830s]</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">natron</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">nitrisch</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:natuurtalent.html>natuurtalent</a> (11191)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:natuur.html>natuur</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:talent.html>talent</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Naturtalent</i>. First attested just after 1800, but only becoming common beginning in the late nineteenth century under the influence of widespread German usage in the performing <a href = vnd.unilang:arts.html>arts</a>.
</p>
